dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// `.meta()` is a convenience method for registering a schema in `z.globalRegistry`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> emailSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">meta</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Email address&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  description: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Your email address&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(emailSchema);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, title: &quot;Email address&quot;, description: &quot;Your email address&quot;, ... } </span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_1fiilubv9fl5b_-trigger-zod-mini" hidden="" id="radix-_R_1fiilubv9fl5b_-content-zod-mini" tabindex="0" class="p-4 prose-no-margin [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:-m-4 [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:rounded-none [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:border-none"></div></div>
<p>All metadata fields get copied into the resulting JSON Schema.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">meta</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  whatever: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">1234</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(schema);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, whatever: 1234 }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="unrepresentable"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=unrepresentable"><code>unrepresentable</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The following APIs are not representable in JSON Schema. By default, Zod will throw an error if they are encountered. It is unsound to attempt a conversion to JSON Schema; you should modify your schemas  as they have no equivalent in JSON. An error will be thrown if any of these are encountered.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">bigint</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">int64</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">symbol</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">void</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">set</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">transform</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">nan</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">custom</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>By default, Zod will throw an error if any of these are encountered.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">bigint</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; throws Error</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>You can change this behavior by setting the <code>unrepresentable</code> option to <code>&quot;any&quot;</code>. This will convert any unrepresentable types to <code>{}</code> (the equivalent of <code>unknown</code> in JSON Schema).</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">bigint</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(), { unrepresentable: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;any&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="cycles"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=cycles"><code>cycles</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>How to handle cycles. If a cycle is encountered as <code>z.toJSONSchema()</code> traverses the schema, it will be represented using <code>$ref</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  get</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> friend</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> User;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(User);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   properties: { name: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; }, friend: { &#x27;$ref&#x27;: &#x27;#&#x27; } },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   required: [ &#x27;name&#x27;, &#x27;friend&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   additionalProperties: false,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>If instead you want to throw an error, set the <code>cycles</code> option to <code>&quot;throw&quot;</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(User, { cycles: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;throw&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; throws Error</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="reused"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=reused"><code>reused</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>How to handle schemas that occur multiple times in the same schema. By default, Zod will inline these schemas.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  firstName: name,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  lastName: name,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(User);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   properties: { </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     firstName: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; }, </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     lastName: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; } </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   required: [ &#x27;firstName&#x27;, &#x27;lastName&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   additionalProperties: false,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Instead you can set the <code>reused</code> option to <code>&quot;ref&quot;</code> to extract these schemas into <code>$defs</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(User, { reused: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;ref&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   properties: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     firstName: { &#x27;$ref&#x27;: &#x27;#/$defs/__schema0&#x27; },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     lastName: { &#x27;$ref&#x27;: &#x27;#/$defs/__schema0&#x27; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   required: [ &#x27;firstName&#x27;, &#x27;lastName&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   additionalProperties: false,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   &#x27;$defs&#x27;: { __schema0: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; } }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="override"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=override"><code>override</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>To define some custom override logic, use <code>override</code>. The provided callback has access to the original Zod schema and the default JSON Schema. <em>This function should directly modify <code>ctx.jsonSchema</code>.</em></p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> mySchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"> /* ... */</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(mySchema, {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  override</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">ctx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ctx.zodSchema; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// the original Zod schema</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ctx.jsonSchema; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// the default JSON Schema</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    // directly modify</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ctx.jsonSchema.whatever </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;sup&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Note that unrepresentable types will throw an <code>Error</code> before this function is called. If you are trying to define custom behavior for an unrepresentable type, you&#x27;ll need to set the <code>unrepresentable: &quot;any&quot;</code> alongside <code>override</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// support z.date() as ISO datetime strings</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(), {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  unrepresentable: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;any&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  override</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">ctx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> def</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ctx.zodSchema._zod.def;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(def.type </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">===</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;date&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">){</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      ctx.jsonSchema.type </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;string&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      ctx.jsonSchema.format </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;date-time&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="conversion"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=conversion">Conversion</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Below are additional details regarding Zod&#x27;s JSON Schema conversion logic.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="string-formats"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=string-formats">String formats</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Zod converts the following schema types to the equivalent JSON Schema <code>format</code>:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Supported via `format`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;email&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">datetime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;date-time&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;date&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">time</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;time&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">duration</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;duration&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ipv4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;ipv4&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ipv6</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;ipv6&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">uuid</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;uuid&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">guid</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;uuid&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">url</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;uri&quot; }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>These schemas are supported via <code>contentEncoding</code>:</p>

[@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">base64</span><span <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">nanoid</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
