<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="numeric-types"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=numeric-types">Numeric types</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Zod converts the following numeric types to JSON Schema:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// number</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;number&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">float32</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;number&quot;, exclusiveMinimum: ..., exclusiveMaximum: ... }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">float64</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;number&quot;, exclusiveMinimum: ..., exclusiveMaximum: ... }</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// integer</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;integer&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">int32</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;integer&quot;, exclusiveMinimum: ..., exclusiveMaximum: ... }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="object-schemas"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=object-schemas">Object schemas</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>By default, <code>z.object()</code> schemas contain <code>additionalProperties: &quot;false&quot;</code>. This is an accurate representation of Zod&#x27;s default behavior, as plain <code>z.object()</code> schema strip additional properties.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  age: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(schema)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   properties: { name: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; }, age: { type: &#x27;number&#x27; } },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   required: [ &#x27;name&#x27;, &#x27;age&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   additionalProperties: false,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>When converting to JSON Schema in <code>&quot;input&quot;</code> mode, <code>additionalProperties</code> is not set. See the <a href="#io"><code>io</code> docs</a> for more information.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  age: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(schema, { io: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;input&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   properties: { name: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; }, age: { type: &#x27;number&#x27; } },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   required: [ &#x27;name&#x27;, &#x27;age&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>By contrast:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>z.looseObject()</code> will <em>never</em> set <code>additionalProperties: false</code></li>
<li><code>z.strictObject()</code> will <em>always</em> set <code>additionalProperties: false</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="file-schemas"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=file-schemas">File schemas</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Zod converts <code>z.file()</code> to the following OpenAPI-friendly schema:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">file</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot;, format: &quot;binary&quot;, contentEncoding: &quot;binary&quot; }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Size and MIME checks are also represented:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">file</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">min</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">max</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">1024</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> 1024</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">mime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;image/png&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   type: &quot;string&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   format: &quot;binary&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   contentEncoding: &quot;binary&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   contentMediaType: &quot;image/png&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   minLength: 1,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   maxLength: 1048576,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="nullability"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=nullability">Nullability</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Zod converts <code>z.null()</code> to <code>{ type: &quot;null&quot; }</code> in JSON Schema.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">null</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;null&quot; }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Note that <code>z.undefined()</code> is unrepresentable in JSON Schema (see <a href="#unrepresentable">below</a>).</p>
<p>Similarly, <code>nullable</code> is represented via a union with <code>null</code>:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">nullable</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { oneOf: [{ type: &quot;string&quot; }, { type: &quot;null&quot; }] }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Optional schemas are represented as-is, though they are decorated with an <code>optional</code> annotation.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">optional</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { type: &quot;string&quot; }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<!-- -->
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="registries"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=registries">Registries</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Passing a schema into <code>z.toJSONSchema()</code> will return a <em>self-contained</em> JSON Schema.</p>
<p>In other cases, you may have a set of Zod schemas you&#x27;d like to represent using multiple interlinked JSON Schemas, perhaps to write to <code>.json</code> files and serve from a web server.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  get</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> posts</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(){</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">array</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(Post);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> Post</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  content: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  get</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> author</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(){</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> User;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.globalRegistry.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">add</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(User, {id: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;User&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.globalRegistry.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">add</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(Post, {id: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Post&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To achieve this, you can pass a <a href="/metadata#registries">registry</a> into <code>z.toJSONSchema()</code>.</p>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p><strong>Important</strong> — All schemas should have a registered <code>id</code> property in the registry! Any schemas without an <code>id</code> will be ignored.</p>
</div></div></div>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.globalRegistry);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   schemas: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     User: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       id: &#x27;User&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       properties: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         name: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         posts: { type: &#x27;array&#x27;, items: { &#x27;$ref&#x27;: &#x27;Post&#x27; } }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       required: [ &#x27;name&#x27;, &#x27;posts&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       additionalProperties: false,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     Post: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       id: &#x27;Post&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       properties: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         title: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         content: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         author: { &#x27;$ref&#x27;: &#x27;User&#x27; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       required: [ &#x27;title&#x27;, &#x27;content&#x27;, &#x27;author&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       additionalProperties: false,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>By default, the <code>$ref</code> URIs are simple relative paths like <code>&quot;User&quot;</code>. To make these absolute URIs, use the <code>uri</code> option. This expects a function that converts an <code>id</code> to a fully-qualified URI.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toJSONSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.globalRegistry, {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  uri</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> `https://example.com/${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">}.json`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   schemas: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     User: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       id: &#x27;User&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       type: &#x27;object&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       properties: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         name: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         posts: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//           type: &#x27;array&#x27;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//           items: { &#x27;$ref&#x27;: &#x27;https://example.com/Post.json&#x27; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       required: [ &#x27;name&#x27;, &#x27;posts&#x27; ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       additionalProperties: false,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     Post: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       id: &#x27;Post&#x27;,</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//         content: { type: &#x27;string&#x27; },</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//       required: [ &#x27;title&#x27;, &#x27;content&#x27;, &#x27;author&#x27; ],</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div role="none" class="flex-1"></div><div class="flex JSON Schema\n\nimport { Tabs, Tab } from 'fumadocs-ui/components/tabs';\nimport { Callout } from \"fumadocs-ui/components/callout\"\nimport { Accordion, Accordions } from 'fumadocs-ui/components/accordion';\n\n\u003cCallout icon={'💎'}\u003e\n  **New** — Zod 4 introduces a new feature: native [JSON Schema](https://json-schema.org/) conversion. JSON Schema is a standard for describing the structure of JSON (with JSON). It's widely used in [OpenAPI](https://www.openapis.org/) definitions and defining [structured outputs](https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/structured-outputs?api-mode=chat) for AI.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\n## `z.fromJSONSchema()`\n\n\u003cCallout type=\"warn\"\u003e\n  **Experimental** — The `z.fromJSONSchema()` function is experimental and is not considered part of Zod's stable API. It is likely to undergo implementation changes in future releases.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\nZod provides `z.fromJSONSchema()` to convert a JSON Schema into a Zod schema.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\n\nconst jsonSchema = {\n  type: \"object\",\n  properties: {\n    name: { type: \"string\" },\n    age: { type: \"number\" },\n  },\n  required: [\"name\", \"age\"],\n};\n\nconst zodSchema = z.fromJSONSchema(jsonSchema);\n```\n\n## `z.toJSONSchema()`\n\nTo convert a Zod schema to JSON Schema, use the `z.toJSONSchema()` function.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\n\nconst schema = z.object({\n  name: z.string(),\n  age: z.number(),\n});\n\nz.toJSONSchema(schema)\n// =\u003e {\n//   type: 'object',\n//   properties: { name: { type: 'string' }, age: { type: 'number' } },\n//   required: [ 'name', 'age' ],\n//   additionalProperties: false,\n// }\n```\n\nAll schema \u0026 checks are converted to their closest JSON Schema equivalent. Some types have no analog and cannot be reasonably represented. See the [`unrepresentable`](#unrepresentable) section below for more information on handling these cases.\n\n```ts\nz.bigint(); // ❌\nz.int64(); // ❌\nz.symbol(); // ❌\nz.undefined(); // ❌\nz.void(); // ❌\nz.date(); // ❌\nz.map(); // ❌\nz.set(); // ❌\nz.transform(); // ❌\nz.nan(); // ❌\nz.custom(); // ❌\n```\n\nA second argument can be used to customize the conversion logic.\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(schema, {\n  // ...params\n})\n```\n\nBelow is a quick reference for each supported parameter. Each one is explained in more detail below.\n\n```ts\ninterface ToJSONSchemaParams {\n  /** The JSON Schema version to target.\n   * - `\"draft-2020-12\"` — Default. JSON Schema Draft 2020-12\n   * - `\"draft-07\"` — JSON Schema Draft 7\n   * - `\"draft-04\"` — JSON Schema Draft 4\n   * - `\"openapi-3.0\"` — OpenAPI 3.0 Schema Object */\n  target?:\n    | \"draft-04\"\n    | \"draft-4\"\n    | \"draft-07\"\n    | \"draft-7\"\n    | \"draft-2020-12\"\n    | \"openapi-3.0\"\n    | ({} \u0026 string)\n    | undefined;\n\n  /** A registry used to look up metadata for each schema. \n   * Any schema with an `id` property will be extracted as a $def. */\n  metadata?: $ZodRegistry\u003cRecord\u003cstring, any\u003e\u003e;\n\n  /** How to handle unrepresentable types.\n   * - `\"throw\"` — Default. Unrepresentable types throw an error\n   * - `\"any\"` — Unrepresentable types become `{}` */\n  unrepresentable?: \"throw\" | \"any\";\n\n  /** How to handle cycles.\n   * - `\"ref\"` — Default. Cycles will be broken using $defs\n   * - `\"throw\"` — Cycles will throw an error if encountered */\n  cycles?: \"ref\" | \"throw\";\n\n  /* How to handle reused schemas.\n   * - `\"inline\"` — Default. Reused schemas will be inlined\n   * - `\"ref\"` — Reused schemas will be extracted as $defs */\n  reused?: \"ref\" | \"inline\";\n\n  /** A function used to convert `id` values to URIs to be used in *external* $refs.\n   *\n   * Default is `(id) =\u003e id`.\n   */\n  uri?: (id: string) =\u003e string;\n}\n```\n\n### `io`\n\nSome schema types have different input and output types, e.g. `ZodPipe`, `ZodDefault`, and coerced primitives. By default, the result of `z.toJSONSchema` represents the *output type*; use `\"io\": \"input\"` to extract the input type instead.\n\n```ts\nconst mySchema = z.string().transform(val =\u003e val.length).pipe(z.number());\n// ZodPipe\n\nconst jsonSchema = z.toJSONSchema(mySchema); \n// =\u003e { type: \"number\" }\n\nconst jsonSchema = z.toJSONSchema(mySchema, { io: \"input\" }); \n// =\u003e { type: \"string\" }\n```\n\n### `target`\n\nTo set the target JSON Schema version, use the `target` parameter. By default, Zod will target Draft 2020-12.\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(schema, { target: \"draft-07\" });\nz.toJSONSchema(schema, { target: \"draft-2020-12\" });\nz.toJSONSchema(schema, { target: \"draft-04\" });\nz.toJSONSchema(schema, { target: \"openapi-3.0\" });\n```\n\n### `metadata`\n\n\u003e If you haven't already, read through the [Metadata and registries](/metadata) page for context on storing metadata in Zod.\n\nIn Zod, metadata is stored in registries. Zod exports a global registry `z.globalRegistry` that can be used to store common metadata fields like `id`, `title`, `description`, and `examples`.\n\n\u003cTabs groupId=\"lib\" items={[\"Zod\", \"Zod Mini\"]}\u003e\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    import * as z from \"zod\";\n\n    // `.meta()` is a convenience method for registering a schema in `z.globalRegistry`\n    const emailSchema = z.string().meta({ \n      title: \"Email address\",\n      description: \"Your email address\",\n    });\n\n    z.toJSONSchema(emailSchema);\n    // =\u003e { type: \"string\", title: \"Email address\", description: \"Your email address\", ... } \n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod Mini\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    import * as z from \"zod\";\n\n    // `.meta()` is a convenience method for registering a schema in `z.globalRegistry`\n    const emailSchema = z.string().register(z.globalRegistry, { \n      title: \"Email address\",\n      description: \"Your email address\",\n    });\n\n    z.toJSONSchema(emailSchema);\n    // =\u003e { type: \"string\", title: \"Email address\", description: \"Your email address\", ... } \n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs\u003e\n\nAll metadata fields get copied into the resulting JSON Schema.\n\n```ts\nconst schema = z.string().meta({\n  whatever: 1234\n});\n\nz.toJSONSchema(schema);\n// =\u003e { type: \"string\", whatever: 1234 }\n```\n\n### `unrepresentable`\n\nThe following APIs are not representable in JSON Schema. By default, Zod will throw an error if they are encountered. It is unsound to attempt a conversion to JSON Schema; you should modify your schemas  as they have no equivalent in JSON. An error will be thrown if any of these are encountered.\n\n```ts\nz.bigint(); // ❌\nz.int64(); // ❌\nz.symbol(); // ❌\nz.undefined(); // ❌\nz.void(); // ❌\nz.date(); // ❌\nz.map(); // ❌\nz.set(); // ❌\nz.transform(); // ❌\nz.nan(); // ❌\nz.custom(); // ❌\n```\n\nBy default, Zod will throw an error if any of these are encountered.\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(z.bigint());\n// =\u003e throws Error\n```\n\nYou can change this behavior by setting the `unrepresentable` option to `\"any\"`. This will convert any unrepresentable types to `{}` (the equivalent of `unknown` in JSON Schema).\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(z.bigint(), { unrepresentable: \"any\" });\n// =\u003e {}\n```\n\n### `cycles`\n\nHow to handle cycles. If a cycle is encountered as `z.toJSONSchema()` traverses the schema, it will be represented using `$ref`.\n\n```ts\nconst User = z.object({\n  name: z.string(),\n  get friend() {\n    return User;\n  },\n});\n\nz.toJSONSchema(User);\n// =\u003e {\n//   type: 'object',\n//   properties: { name: { type: 'string' }, friend: { '$ref': '#' } },\n//   required: [ 'name', 'friend' ],\n//   additionalProperties: false,\n// }\n```\n\nIf instead you want to throw an error, set the `cycles` option to `\"throw\"`.\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(User, { cycles: \"throw\" });\n// =\u003e throws Error\n```\n\n### `reused`\n\nHow to handle schemas that occur multiple times in the same schema. By default, Zod will inline these schemas.\n\n```ts\nconst name = z.string();\nconst User = z.object({\n  firstName: name,\n  lastName: name,\n});\n\nz.toJSONSchema(User);\n// =\u003e {\n//   type: 'object',\n//   properties: { \n//     firstName: { type: 'string' }, \n//     lastName: { type: 'string' } \n//   },\n//   required: [ 'firstName', 'lastName' ],\n//   additionalProperties: false,\n// }\n```\n\nInstead you can set the `reused` option to `\"ref\"` to extract these schemas into `$defs`.\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(User, { reused: \"ref\" });\n// =\u003e {\n//   type: 'object',\n//   properties: {\n//     firstName: { '$ref': '#/$defs/__schema0' },\n//     lastName: { '$ref': '#/$defs/__schema0' }\n//   },\n//   required: [ 'firstName', 'lastName' ],\n//   additionalProperties: false,\n//   '$defs': { __schema0: { type: 'string' } }\n// }\n```\n\n### `override`\n\nTo define some custom override logic, use `override`. The provided callback has access to the original Zod schema and the default JSON Schema. *This function should directly modify `ctx.jsonSchema`.*\n\n```ts\nconst mySchema = /* ... */\nz.toJSONSchema(mySchema, {\n  override: (ctx)=\u003e{\n    ctx.zodSchema; // the original Zod schema\n    ctx.jsonSchema; // the default JSON Schema\n\n    // directly modify\n    ctx.jsonSchema.whatever = \"sup\";\n  }\n});\n```\n\nNote that unrepresentable types will throw an `Error` before this function is called. If you are trying to define custom behavior for an unrepresentable type, you'll need to set the `unrepresentable: \"any\"` alongside `override`.\n\n```ts\n// support z.date() as ISO datetime strings\nconst result = z.toJSONSchema(z.date(), {\n  unrepresentable: \"any\",\n  override: (ctx) =\u003e {\n    const def = ctx.zodSchema._zod.def;\n    if(def.type ===\"date\"){\n      ctx.jsonSchema.type = \"string\";\n      ctx.jsonSchema.format = \"date-time\";\n    }\n  },\n});\n```\n\n## Conversion\n\nBelow are additional details regarding Zod's JSON Schema conversion logic.\n\n### String formats\n\nZod converts the following schema types to the equivalent JSON Schema `format`:\n\n```ts\n// Supported via `format`\nz.email(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"email\" }\nz.iso.datetime(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"date-time\" }\nz.iso.date(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"date\" }\nz.iso.time(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"time\" }\nz.iso.duration(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"duration\" }\nz.ipv4(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"ipv4\" }\nz.ipv6(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"ipv6\" }\nz.uuid(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"uuid\" }\nz.guid(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"uuid\" }\nz.url(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"uri\" }\n```\n\nThese schemas are supported via `contentEncoding`:\n\n```ts\nz.base64(); // =\u003e { type: \"string\", contentEncoding: \"base64\" }\n```\n\nAll other string formats are supported via `pattern`:\n\n```ts\nz.base64url();\nz.cuid();\nz.emoji();\nz.nanoid();\nz.cuid2();\nz.ulid();\nz.cidrv4();\nz.cidrv6();\nz.mac();\n```\n\n### Numeric types\n\nZod converts the following numeric types to JSON Schema:\n\n```ts\n// number\nz.number(); // =\u003e { type: \"number\" }\nz.float32(); // =\u003e { type: \"number\", exclusiveMinimum: ..., exclusiveMaximum: ... }\nz.float64(); // =\u003e { type: \"number\", exclusiveMinimum: ..., exclusiveMaximum: ... }\n\n// integer\nz.int(); // =\u003e { type: \"integer\" }\nz.int32(); // =\u003e { type: \"integer\", exclusiveMinimum: ..., exclusiveMaximum: ... }\n```\n\n### Object schemas\n\nBy default, `z.object()` schemas contain `additionalProperties: \"false\"`. This is an accurate representation of Zod's default behavior, as plain `z.object()` schema strip additional properties.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\n\nconst schema = z.object({\n  name: z.string(),\n  age: z.number(),\n});\n\nz.toJSONSchema(schema)\n// =\u003e {\n//   type: 'object',\n//   properties: { name: { type: 'string' }, age: { type: 'number' } },\n//   required: [ 'name', 'age' ],\n//   additionalProperties: false,\n// }\n```\n\nWhen converting to JSON Schema in `\"input\"` mode, `additionalProperties` is not set. See the [`io` docs](#io) for more information.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\n\nconst schema = z.object({\n  name: z.string(),\n  age: z.number(),\n});\n\nz.toJSONSchema(schema, { io: \"input\" });\n// =\u003e {\n//   type: 'object',\n//   properties: { name: { type: 'string' }, age: { type: 'number' } },\n//   required: [ 'name', 'age' ],\n// }\n```\n\nBy contrast:\n\n* `z.looseObject()` will *never* set `additionalProperties: false`\n* `z.strictObject()` will *always* set `additionalProperties: false`\n\n### File schemas\n\nZod converts `z.file()` to the following OpenAPI-friendly schema:\n\n```ts\nz.file();\n// =\u003e { type: \"string\", format: \"binary\", contentEncoding: \"binary\" }\n```\n\nSize and MIME checks are also represented:\n\n```ts\nz.file().min(1).max(1024 * 1024).mime(\"image/png\");\n// =\u003e {\n//   type: \"string\",\n//   format: \"binary\",\n//   contentEncoding: \"binary\",\n//   contentMediaType: \"image/png\",\n//   minLength: 1,\n//   maxLength: 1048576,\n// }\n```\n\n### Nullability\n\nZod converts `z.null()` to `{ type: \"null\" }` in JSON Schema.\n\n```ts\nz.null();\n// =\u003e { type: \"null\" }\n```\n\nNote that `z.undefined()` is unrepresentable in JSON Schema (see [below](#unrepresentable)).\n\nSimilarly, `nullable` is represented via a union with `null`:\n\n```ts\nz.nullable(z.string());\n// =\u003e { oneOf: [{ type: \"string\" }, { type: \"null\" }] }\n```\n\nOptional schemas are represented as-is, though they are decorated with an `optional` annotation.\n\n```ts\nz.optional(z.string());\n// =\u003e { type: \"string\" }\n```\n\n{/* ### Pipes\n\n  Pipes contain an input and an output schema. Zod uses the *output schema* for JSON Schema conversion. */}\n\n## Registries\n\nPassing a schema into `z.toJSONSchema()` will return a *self-contained* JSON Schema.\n\nIn other cases, you may have a set of Zod schemas you'd like to represent using multiple interlinked JSON Schemas, perhaps to write to `.json` files and serve from a web server.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\n\nconst User = z.object({\n  name: z.string(),\n  get posts(){\n    return z.array(Post);\n  }\n});\n\nconst Post = z.object({\n  title: z.string(),\n  content: z.string(),\n  get author(){\n    return User;\n  }\n});\n\nz.globalRegistry.add(User, {id: \"User\"});\nz.globalRegistry.add(Post, {id: \"Post\"});\n```\n\nTo achieve this, you can pass a [registry](/metadata#registries) into `z.toJSONSchema()`.\n\n\u003e **Important** — All schemas should have a registered `id` property in the registry! Any schemas without an `id` will be ignored.\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(z.globalRegistry);\n// =\u003e {\n//   schemas: {\n//     User: {\n//       id: 'User',\n//       type: 'object',\n//       properties: {\n//         name: { type: 'string' },\n//         posts: { type: 'array', items: { '$ref': 'Post' } }\n//       },\n//       required: [ 'name', 'posts' ],\n//       additionalProperties: false,\n//     },\n//     Post: {\n//       id: 'Post',\n//       type: 'object',\n//       properties: {\n//         title: { type: 'string' },\n//         content: { type: 'string' },\n//         author: { '$ref': 'User' }\n//       },\n//       required: [ 'title', 'content', 'author' ],\n//       additionalProperties: false,\n//     }\n//   }\n// }\n```\n\nBy default, the `$ref` URIs are simple relative paths like `\"User\"`. To make these absolute URIs, use the `uri` option. This expects a function that converts an `id` to a fully-qualified URI.\n\n```ts\nz.toJSONSchema(z.globalRegistry, {\n  uri: (id) =\u003e `https://example.com/${id}.json`\n});\n// =\u003e {\n//   schemas: {\n//     User: {\n//       id: 'User',\n//       type: 'object',\n//       properties: {\n//         name: { type: 'string' },\n//         posts: {\n//           type: 'array',\n//           items: { '$ref': 'https://example.com/Post.json' }\n//         }\n//       },\n//       required: [ 'name', 'posts' ],\n//       additionalProperties: false,\n//     },\n//     Post: {\n//       id: 'Post',\n//       type: 'object',\n//       properties: {\n//         title: { type: 'string' },\n//         content: { type: 'string' },\n//         author: { '$ref': 'https://example.com/User.json' }\n//       },\n//       required: [ 'title', 'content', 'author' ],\n//       additionalProperties: false,\n//     }\n//   }\n// }\n```\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"26:[\"$\",\"$L32\",null,{\"toc\":[{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#zfromjsonschema\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"z.fromJSONSchema()\"}]},{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#ztojsonschema\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"z.toJSONSchema()\"}]},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#io\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"io\"}]},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#target\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"target\"}]},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#metadata\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"metadata\"}]},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#unrepresentable\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"unrepresentable\"}]},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#cycles\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"cycles\"}]},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#reused\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"reused\"}]},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#override\",\"title\":[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"override\"}]},{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#conversion\",\"title\":\"Conversion\"},{\"depth\":3,\"url\":\"#string-formats\",\"title\":\"String
